< Review>
The remodel looks nice. It isn't as cramped as before. It looks clean. Not all the nail techs offer or bring their clients water.

I walk through the front door and I am greeted to see what I need to get done. Then I get seated in the middle chair in the first row. This lady took a while to get situated because a young lady who came in after me was getting started on her acrylic nails. If acrylic nails are a priority, don't offer other services.

The lady that was doing my nails sat their quietly did my nails until I started seeing bubbles because she was rushing through the shellac gel and messed up. Don't get me wrong. She did an 80% job overall, but it should be 100% all the time every time. She should get all flustered because she messed up and I asked her to fix it. If she did it right the first time, there would be no need for her to fix it and be all rough with my hands. In the end, two nails were messed up. She didn't cover the entire nail that she messed up on  There was a dark lint on my other finger. Lastly, there were tiny bubbles on a couple of other fingers.

As the last set was setting under the UV light, she was pressing for some lotion; unfortunately, the bottle was out and she only rubbed the teeny tiny bit of lotion that came out of the bottle on top of my hand and rubbed it in circles and that was it. I had to ask her for the cuticle oil and she asked some if I wanted to wipe my hands down. I really wanted to ask her what was included in the gel package because all I received was a little bit of filing, cuticles cut, cuticle oil, and shellac gel with a "splash" of lotion for the something not even close to a massage that is normally offered. If she was in training, she should be supervised better or let alone retrained.

Not having her do my nails again. Too bad they don't have name badges anymore because I wouldn't recommend her until she gets better training and customer service. Keep in mind that I did tipped her though!<//Review>

< text>
Extremely underhanded business. I went in to buy some tubes for my girlfriend, and the receipt that I got with the tubes said that "all sales on rubber final" however; that was not communicated to me BEFORE I bought the tubes. When I told my GF how much I had spent, (almost $50 for 4 tubes!) she went online to compare pricing and realized they were priced at literally 3 times the amount of comparable tubes from Jenson USA. I went back to pedals to let them know and return the tubes only to be pulled outside the shop like a child and have the owner start to argue with me about his business expenses. He admitted to me the only reason he doesn't want to return rubber or tubes is because of the 3% return fee that credit card processing companies charge him! What a way to put your customers first huh? He offered me store credit but I at that point did not want to spend another minute in that shop nor will I ever again. They lost my business and recommendation to friends looking to buy a $3,000+ MTB. Too bad! The bottom line is that if they do not offer Returns on certain products they should be informing customers of which products those are before the transaction is completed. End of story. This is an extremely underhanded and dishonest policy to abide by and based on that principal alone, I will never set foot in that shop again or recommend their business to anyone else who rides bicycles.<//text>

< Text>
This shop really is for everyone, from the cycle enthusiast to the beginner, like me, just starting out. The guys that work there took really good care of me when I purchased one of their new "Giant" road bicycles, a helmet and a light set. My wife bought hers there a couple months back and highly recommended I check them out. An hour after I made my purchase, my bike was perfectly tuned and ready to go! Well, about a month after my purchase I acquired a flat, I took my bike back in there and the owner himself hooked me up with everything I needed to get me moving again as well as took the extra time to hip me to some things about how to better lessen my chances of future flats. I will always recommend this awesome little shop to anyone looking to buy a bike or accessories or even just to ask questions about the sport as they all ride from what I gathered and really know their stuff. From my family to yours, a loyal customer for life, thanks to everyone at Pedals Bike shop, wishing you many years of success!< /Text>
